12-06-19-20-06
At give afkald på frugten af sine handlinger er karma yoga. Karma yoga går hånd i hånd med at se
sig selv ske, at dæmpe aktiviteten i de selvrefererende funktionelle netværk. At give afkald på
frugten af sine handlinger går hånd i hånd med at give slip på fremtiden, både frygten og håbet.
Karma yoga er derfor en integreret del af at være til stede i nuet, at mærke og sanse bevidsthedens
indhold, at hvile i bevidstheden selv. Jeg har ikke dyb kendskab til hinduistisk tankegang om
karma, blot ved jeg, at hvis karma skal forstås som relateret til genfødsel eller som en generel
term for transempiriske årsag-effekt forhold, så har jeg ikke nogen baggrund for at lade karma
være en del af mit metafysiske perspektiv. Jeg antager, at karma generelt antages på baggrund af
hellige skrifter, som jeg ikke anser for at være åbenbarede. Alt dette siger jeg egentlig blot for
at komme med den pointe, at karma yoga som beskrevet, ikke kræver en tro på karma, men kan blive
hjulpet på vej ved en benægtelse af den frie vilje, der ikke kan opretholdes uden troen på det
separate selv. Ved at betragte alle fænomeners essensløshed, deres distribuerethed i rummet, mister
også kroppen og sindets bevægelser det centrum, der skulle være deres kilde. Karma yoga er altså
den konkrete praksis, de momenter i vores liv, hvor vi opdager at vi er bundet til udfaldet af
vores handlinger, at vi regner med dem, at vi ængstes over dem, at vi ikke er i nuet og vil lade
i morgen være i morgen. Diskussionen om fri vilje er derimod et intellektuelt metafysisk problem,
der dog kan være hjælpsom, ved at give indsigt og hjælpe med at acceptere selve praksissen af
karma yogaen.

Min meditation fokuserer nu på samadhi, fordi jeg læste om en undersøgelse med hjernescanninger
af folk der skulle genkalde spirituelle oplevelser, der viste øget aktivitet i centre relateret
til koncentration og dæmpet aktivitet i centre relateret til selvreference. Se forrige indlæg
for uddybning af tanken om, at spiritualitet i høj grad handler om at opøve evner og en
neurofysiologi der understøtter dem. Maharshi siger, at self-enquiry kun er for den modne aspirant,
der allerede har øvet sig i yoga, hvormed han især mener samadhi ved hjælp af pranayama. Jeg
fokuserer på en generel mindfulness i mit aktive liv og på samadhi i min meditation. Jeg har haft
gode resultater i dag; det går godt med at stilne aktiviteten i selvet og være hurtig til at fange
de større afvigelser fra fokusset, som især har været næsebor. Jeg eksperimenterer dog med en
blanding af ren anapanasati, hvor der ingen kontrol af åndedrættet er, og så en slags pranayama,
idet jeg forsøger at stilne åndedrættet og gøre det langtrukkent, men på en rimelig intuitiv måde,
hvor jeg gradvist føler mig frem til et afdæmpet sind.

Jeg sigter generelt efter den første jhana,
som beskrevet af Brasington, ved at flytte fokus til mine læber. Jeg tror dog at jeg er hindret af
to ting; jeg bliver forventningsfuld, når jeg laver bevægelsen, fordi jeg nu begynder at tænke på,
hvordan det vil blive: Brasington beskriver det sådan at den behagelige følelse, piti, der er på
læben eller hænderne eller hvor man nu vælger at have sit fokus, ville vokse og blive mere generel
og til sidst eksplodere i piti. Det er ikke mærkeligt, at man bliver forventningsfuld af dette.
Jeg gad vide, hvor stort det rum af strategier for at bevæge sig igennem de jhanaer som Brasington
identificerer mon er? Eller mere generelt: Kan man konceptualisere sindstilstande i et komplekst
faserum, og i så fald, hvor snævre er vejene mellem disse? Hvordan skal man visuelt forestille sig
et faserum, hvor det er svært at nå direkte til fx lige præcis den sjette jhana fra normal
meditationskoncentration? Hvor bred er jhanaen? Hvor uniform er den, hvad er topologien, er der
en glidende overgang eller en brat overgang? Alt dette vil være spændende at undersøge, hvis
neurovidenskabens teknologier bliver bedre. Jeg er dog begyndt at håbe mindre på videnskaben, al
dens aktivitet er forgængelige fænomener, og jeg er blevet bevidst om at jeg har været for knyttet
til den. Måske er den erfarne spirituelle praktisør en der har generel erfaring med dette indre
terræn, øver sig i at passere gennem terrænet, at blive i bestemte tilstande et givent stykke tid
og smidigt bevæger sig igennem det som en gymnast.

Det blev et sidespor, angående forhindringen i at komme dertil: Den anden forhindring er, at jeg
to gange, hvor jeg har flyttet fokusset til læberne har mærket piti i mine kønsorganer og begyndende
rejsning. Jeg tror jeg vil sige det sådan, at noget af mig tolker det som seksuel opstemmelse og
det er en selvopfyldende profeti, fordi det frembringer billeder, der får mig til at miste min
koncentration. Det er nu over ti dage siden jeg sidst har haft orgasme, og i dag er første dag,
hvor jeg har haft nogen lyst, men den er til gengæld stærk nu.

10-06-19-19-18
Spirituelle praksisser er formentlig opøvelse af neurale strukturer.
Plasticiteten giver håb: Den spirituelle praksis er muligheden for at et menneske kan have
det godt. Jeg har ingen ontologiske dogmer at holde fast på. Kun et ego kan have sådanne.
Sandheden er ikke vigtig at have. Et menneske kan kun have sandhed ved at holde det i sin
hjerne, men hjernen og kroppen er forgængelig. Sandt er sandt, om det kendes eller ej.
Al meditation, der bygger på mantraer, vil nok blot resultere i at den mediterende finder det,
han eller hun allerede forventer at se. Der intet galt i det, men jeg tror ikke jeg vil følge 
Maharshis "Hvem er jeg?", da det binder mig til en monistisk ontologi. Jeg er ikke bange for at
tage fejl, jeg er bange for at mit ego,er urent begær efter at have ret, at have sandhed. Et begær, der må lægges til side.
Jeg ved ikke om det er Advaita eller Buddhisme eller noget tredje, der har hvad jeg har brug for.
Det er ikke vigtigt for mig, hvad der er i stedet for egoet, kun at der gives et alternativ til
egoet. Når egoet svinder hen, når det falder til ro er der en fred. Denne fred behøver ikke at
have nogen dyb ontologisk signifikans. Jeg tror mange forskellige sprituelle traditioner finder
forskellige avancerede sindstilstande, der er udgør modgift til den miserable ego, til den
grundlæggende stress. Disse sindstilstande er indlejret i traditionerne, der tolker dem og sætter
ord på dem. Disse tolkninger er ikke blot epifænomener, der frit kan ignoreres, for ordene har magt,
både til at lede ved instrukser og til at give billeder, der kan hjælpe på vej. De understøtter og
muliggør replikationen af en opøvet neuralitet fra et menneske til et andet. Jeg tror dog at
erfaring med et sæt teknikker kan overføres til et andet, og på den måde er der ikke den store
fare i at give sig i kast med en teknik: Ikke blot, er det ikke nødvendigt at være nervøs for,
at den filosofi, der ligger bag, skulle være forkert, fra den vinkel jeg lige har præsenteret, men
erfaringen ville sandsynligvis også være brugbar i en anden kontekst. Et problem ser jeg her;
fristelsen til at egoet binder sig fast til tanken om at være en spirituel virtuoso. Dette er
paradoksalt: Virtuøsiteten ville bestå i at aflægge og dæmpe egoet.

Nedergaard. Jacob kom og lavede et halshug tegn, for at indikere at Nedergaard nok var sur. Der
var en slags valgaften i en gade om aftenen, og noget med klima. Jeg var sammen med nogle folk
på min egen alder, og en af dem var formand for noget, og på et tidspunkt stod han på gaden og
fortalte noget. Han refererede til et eller andet meget praktisk, for eksempel et toilet eller
noget andet man ville have kendsskab til hvis man havde håndværkerviden. Tidligere var jeg sammen
med Mads, min grandfætter, og min far. Jeg talte om Adveita-Vedanta i lang tid, det var ikke en
samtale, fordi jeg snakkede i så lang tid.

Alle disse drømme er blot fænomener, former der dukker op i sindet. Jeg prøver ikke at huske dem,
fordi jeg tror de betyder noget, fordi de er vigtige, eller fordi jeg tror der er noget at hente.
Men idet man kan øge sin luciditet i drømmene, bliver man bedre til at skue igennem det store
skuespil, hvirvelvinden af fænomener, og jeg tror den er god at have: Det er når man ser verden
i vågen tilstand som noget der minder om en drøm, at man kan undgå at identificere med det. Man
kan se at det hele er uvirkeligt i den simple forstand at det er fundamntalt midlertidigt og
begrænset. At føle at verden i vågen tilstand er som en drøm, er ikke at sige, at det er en slags
drøm, eller en simulering, eller at den ikke er virkelig. Det er i stedet en tanke, der introducerer
et begreb om luciditet ind i det vågne liv: Du kan være fuldstændig fanget af drømmen, du
falder ned i den, du krummer dig sammen, dit hjerte begynder at banke, du tror du skal dø. Du kan
dog også være lucid, og se at det blot er en drøm, at der intet er at frygte, at alt er som det
er, at du ikke kan dø. Det er noget af den slags luciditet, jeg gerne vil fostre i mit eget liv.

Da jeg havde min dårlige oplevelse i gymnasiet, med depersonalisation/derealisation, følte og
tænkte jeg distinkt, at det hele var som i en drøm. Det kan dog ikke have været det, der gjorde
at det var en negativ oplevelse. Selvom nogle spirituelle traditioner vil have deres fortolkning
af DP/DR, så er det jo også et psykologisk fænomen, og jeg har tænkt det som en psykose. Jeg tror
det giver mening at tænke DP/DR som en reaktion på stress, hvor det psykologiske system finder
et slags optimum, hvor der laves en skarp skelnen mellem selvet og verden. Eckhart Tolle, en
tysk spirituel lærer, har beskrevet at han var i dyb depression og sagde til sig selv: "Jeg kan
ikke leve med mig selv mere!" og begyndte at tænkt på den dualitet der er i den sætning "jeg" og
"mig", og at han forstår det der skete med ham som et split mellem egoet og bevidsthed. Maharshi
skulle også have haft sin fundamentale hændelse, da han som barn troede at han skulle dø: Han
accepterede det, men ville finde ud af, hvad det var der skulle dø. Det er forståeligt, at
Maharshis self-inquiry går ud på at spørge "hvem er jeg?". Man kan hypotetisere, at disse åndelige
hændelser som mennesker har, er en slags psykologiske nedbrud, der i stedet for at gå helt galt,
resulterer i noget godt og gavnligt, at disidentificeringen med egoet er en psykologisk
forsvarsmekanisme, der er adaptiv på organismens plan.

Det går fint fremad med rapporten til SU eksamen. Da jeg kom hjem så jeg en video med Poonja.
Han gav et godt indtryk af Selvet, og den frihed der er i Selvet: Der intet i fænomenernes og
formernes verden, der kan tilfredsstille, det er alt sammen midlertidigt, men det smukkeste af
alt er til stede, det er ikke fundet i verden, det kan ikke peges på, ja det måske overhovedet
ingen ting. Når du kigger ind i dig selv, for at finde ud af hvem du er vil du blot finde denne
tomhed, der alligevel har en sådan enorm fylde. Idet vi længes efter ydre fænomener, ydre lykke
slører vi denne glans. Der er intet problem i dette, Selvet er det eneste. Visdommen, den eneste
visdom er at tage denne perle som det eneste, at kaste sig i armene på friheden.

Det jeg synes er interessant, og som jeg reflekterer over, er hvad sammenhængen er mellem at
identificere sig med bevidsthed i stedet for sin person og så det psykologiske helbred for denne
person, og mere generelt dets neurokemi. Jeg har lyst til at kramme de folk jeg ser. Jeg antager
at dette betyder, at jeg har et øget oxytocinniveau. Jeg kommer til at tænke på en sommer i
Italien, hvor jeg var i en lykkelig sindstilstand, der var meget lig den jeg er i nu. Jeg fortolkede
den på det tidspunkt som Helligåndens stærke tilstedeværelse. Det der kendetegner begge tilstande
er en form for koncentration, der ikke gælder på kortere sigt, altså fra sekund til sekund, men
snarere minut til minut. Der er naturligvis ikke blot tale om fokus, der er også noget andet. Det
er imidlertid interessant, at jeg forbinder min nuværende tilstand med en form for ikke-dualistisk
fortolkning, mens det på ingen måde kan have været tilfældet på det tidspunkt, fordi jeg ingen
kendsskab havde til sådan tankegang på det tidspunkt. Er det blot sommeren, der er kommet over
mig? Det kan ikke være den eneste faktor, i tilfældet at sommeren er en vigtig faktor, er det
blot det: En vigtig faktor. Udover min sindstilstand, tror jeg, jeg er ved at have et paradigmatisk
skift også intellektuelt: Jeg har i lang tid været materialist i forhold til psykisk liv og velvære,
på en sådan måde at jeg har fokuseret meget på neurokemi og ment at fysisk sundhed, heriblandt
træning og kost, ville være den fundamentale faktor for psykisk sundhed og kreativ udfoldelse. Det
handler ikke om, at jeg ikke længere anerkender at dette er en vigtig faktor, jeg tror bare at jeg
har lukket øjnene for ideen om psykoterapi og hvordan vores tilgang til verden har enorm betydning
for vores psykiske liv og velvære. I stedet for at det skulle være sommeren eller nogen anden
specifik faktor, tror jeg snarere jeg er havnet i en heldig matrix, hvor jeg har fået øjnene op
for dette, i kraft af den stress, depression og angst, jeg har følt, den utilfredshed jeg har
følt, der har ledt mig ind i et krydsfelt, der har faciliteret en forandring. Der hersker en
smule tvivl og frygt for at dette måtte forsvinde, og hvis man skulle sammenligne med de kristne
oplevelser, har jeg jo haft samme tanke: Jeg vil aldrig stoppe med at have det sådan her. Men denne
frygt kommer fra egoet, der tænker over sin egen fremtid og sit velbefindende. Jeg tror egoet er
selve forbandelsen, der kommer intet godt ud af at leve sig ind i denne frygt, og det vil den
metakognitive terapi også sige.

Der er en verden, der flyder rundt, og der er materie, der strækkes og slippes, der er spædning,
der opbygges og aftager, bygger op og falder sammen. Jeg er borte, så snart, ligesom alle jeg
kender og alt jeg har set. Alt hvad mine tanker referer til at betingede fænomener, og det gør
mig ikke ked af det. Det var Samsara, der fik mig til at tænke på bølgerne og bevægelsen og at
der er så mange ting, der ser faste ud for os, men de er selv flydende på længere sigt. Samsara
og Baraka er fantastiske film, der er en del af mit nuværende krydsfelt. Jeg føler lige nu, at
jeg er meget højere end jeg er. Jeg vil gerne tale om perspektiv. Douglas Harding beskriver
ifølge Sam Harris, Dzogchen for et vestligt publikum. Jeg så en video med Harding, hvor han
taler om at være hovedløs. At opdage, at man ikke kan se sit eget hoved er en simpel måde, hvorpå
man kan blive hjulpet til at lægge mærke til sit eget førstepersonsperspektiv, og derved begyndte
at se bevidsthed som sådan, man kan begynde at være bevidst om at man er bevidst, man kan begynde
at se Seeren, den umådeligt smukke Seer. Der er intet mystisk i at man ikke kan se sit eget
ansigt, der er intet mystisk i at man har et perspektiv, hvorfra man kan høre visse ting og ikke
andre, hvorfra man kan se andre ting og ikke se andre. Der er et stort aspekt af dette, der er
ren optik og geometri. Jeg har tænkt på det, men har aldrig kommet videre; jeg vil gerne tale
om information. Der er noget information, der når mig, og andet der ikke gør.

Jeg har haft det rigtig godt siden i forgårs aften. Jeg læste om Ramana Maharshi, en indisk mand,
der kategoriseres som Advaita-Vedanata, ikke-dualisme. Han talte om Selvet, som han så ved at

kommer ved at identificere mig med Kasper, med min krop, med min begrænsede materielle eksistens.
Det er håbløst, da dette liv med sikkerhed vil ende. Det er håbløst, da det begrænsede jeg, egoet,
aldrig kan blive tilfreds. Det er håbløst, da egoet ikke er forskelligt fra verden. Jeg vil hellere
identificere mig med bevidstheden, der oplever alt. Jeg vil hellere identificere mig med det rum,
hvori tankerne opstår, end tankerne selv. Jeg vil hellere identificere mig med verden, uafhængig
af dens nuværende form og konstitution. Jeg kan mærke det tydeligt, at de fleste tankerrækker, som
jeg falder ned i, straks begynder at opbygge egoet med dets frygt og dets adskillelse fra verden,
og at det knuger i mit hjerte, når det sker. Jeg vil gerne vende mig til at være hurtig til at
mærke denne knugen, mærke den lidelse som jeg påfører mig selv, og derefter give slip og returnere
til det der ikke kan lide, blive i det store selv, den klare og tomme bevidsthed, intetheden, der
ikke er bundet af noget nuværende. Jeg kan mærke at jeg i går havde meget mere kærlighed til de
mennesker der er omkring mig, når jeg identificerede med dem, når jeg lod det være min identitet,
frem for Kasper. Kasper i sig selv er blot et enkelt menneske, der vil være borte snarligt. Der
er absolut intet at opnå. Bevidstheden selv, væren selv er den rene lykke. Jeg er blevet drevet
til dette, fordi jeg ikke kan holde til at være en Kasper, hvis lykke er afhængig af at det skal
gå perfekt akademisk, at det skal gå godt i fremtiden, at der ikke skal være folk, der hader ham,

der havde frembragt hans liv nok skulle sørge for at dets livsforløb. Hvorfor skulle jeg bekymre
mig for i morgen? I morgen skal nok ske. Og det kan være det går galt i morgen, eller det kan
være det gik galt i går. Men det kan ikke gå galt for selvet. Det kan gå galt for Kasper. Så selv
hvis frygten og angsten havde et fornuftigt grundlag, ville det ikke være fornuftigt at leve sig
selv ind i den og ødelægge livet for sig selv endnu mere. Jeg skal huske at skrive, for det er

Jeg tror meget af det handler om, at man selvom det lyder det umiddelbart lyder usundt, at man skal
adskille sig selv, man skal lave et split i sit sind mellem sit ego og sin bevidsthed. Alt indhold
i bevidstheden har stadig et perspektiv, al erfaring ses fra dette perspektiv, men det er lige

31-05-19-10-10
Connectionism describes cognition as the result of the a generalised network structure where
the different components of cognition emerge from the same basic neural building blocks. This
results in a view of cognition in which thoughts, beliefs, memories, plans and other elements
of cognition cannot fully be regarded as discrete objects.

It seems to me that there are interesting ground between connectionism and mindfulness. A
part of the buddhist mindfulness philosophy is the awareness of the contents of consciousness
without attributing permanence or essence to these elements. In the Vipassana tradition there
is the notion that sensations will have to be broken down into smaller parts until it one is
able to feel are more raw type of sensation. Vipassana has a strong focus on bodily sensation.
Goenkas belief is that by doing the body scanning, thoughts will emerge some of which are
deeper than others, but that one should not react and engage with these. In more generalised
mindfulness, mindfulness can be applied to consciousness in general, not merely the sensations
of the body, but all signals appearing in consciousness. By training present moment awareness
it is possible to gain a more detailed picture of consciousness, both statically and dynamically;
consciousness has a certain width in the sense that there exists multiple signals at the same
time at different parts of the body. A lot of different signals are present in the brain, even
though one might argue that it not possibl to talk about different signals, and that the perceived
difference between signals emerge from a lack of understanding of the oneness of these signals.
For pragmatic purposes, however, it is meaningful to speak of a variety of signals and different
senses.

Thus there is a width and it will be possible to train the ability to concentrate and
be aware of the width of consciousness, but a perhaps more important aspect is the temporal
dimension. The meditator will be able to get a better understanding of thoughts in general and
how they follow each other; the how and what of distraction. Fx associationism in which the
sequence of thoughts are thought to arise by having one thought in which some elements leads one
to think of another thought containing or having similar elements to those elements etc. Even
though associationism is perhaps a very simplistic conceptualisation of cognition, there is
undoubtedly some aspects of it which is meaningful. The mediatator will practice the awareness
of these movements between thoughts and will perhaps have experiential knowledge of thoughts
and non-discrete entities; that there is not really a sequence of distinct though objects, but
that consciousness contains a large continuous flow. It is here associationism bridges with
connectionism.

It is hard to deny that there is also a hierarchical aspect to cognition especially
regarding planning which has a strong influence on the contents of thoughts and what thoughts
appear. The associations which lead one onto another thought is not merely based on the objective
statistical similarity between to memories or ideas. This similarity will be multiplied with the
importance. Thus one might find cycles of thoughts, repeatedly focusing on specific past or
future events. These events will have certain importance but also a charge in the sense of being
positive or negative or perhaps the charge has a more complex structure than a simple scalar.
Goenka and much buddhist thought will claim that when a thought arises there is a certain
reaction to this based on the positivity or negativity of the thought and that the cultivation
of equanimity is completely fundamental to the project of meditation: The emotional engagement
with the thoughts is a feedback process in which one further amplifies the negativity of the
memory and increases its power such that when it occurs in the mind another time, it will be
even more negativity. However, the same holds for positive thoughts; buddhism advocates that
one does not cling to the pleasantness of thoughts because one develops a dependency which cannot
be upheld in impermanent world. When the pleasantness is not present one will miss it and negativity
will arise from this longing. We see how Vipassana relates sensation and thought. When being aware
of the sensations in the body one practices the same non-reactive sentiment as one does to the
thoughts, perhaps because these thoughts are nothing but more vague signals than the actual present
signal. The reaction to the sensations in the present constitute an evaluation of the present
moment which will be the basis for the charge as it is stored in memory.

The actual structure of a reaction is not explained in much detail in Vipassana, and perhaps it
is here metacognitive behavioral therapy and the concept of self-regulatory executive function
is relevant. When a thought arises as a signal in consciousness, lack of mindfulness will lead
one to engage with the thought as if though it was present. One is immersed into the thought as
if though it is really present and engaging with the emotions one might feel in that situation.
These emotions are not merely mental but have a strong bodily component. The fear, the happiness,
the worry, the sadness will be felt in the body, even though it is not clear what it means; it
could be that there is an actual change occuring in the body or the signal could be an imitation
of the bodily sensations but which are only present in the brain. Most likely both cases are
true. It is clear that often the body is changed: Heart rate can rise, cringing of the feet can
occur, jitters occur in muscles and so on. Notice that there cannot be any such thing as a purely
phantomic sensation, it is a matter of distance or width; in which area of the nervous system and
body does the feeling occur.

Baraka.

Livet er kort og alting flyder. Der er intet at holde fast i, så det er bedst at give slip.
Hvordan kan jeg leve mere simpelt? Hvordan kan jeg lev i det samfund, jeg lever i, og stadig
bevare min frihed? Der er så ekstremt mange mennesker på denne jord, og de lever så forskellige
liv fra mig. Det må jeg ikke glemme og jeg må ikke glemme døden. Jeg må ikke glemme at kloden
er en enkelt klode og at universet er ufatteligt. Hold sindet simpelt, ryd op i dit sind, pas
på med hvilke signaler du giver lov til at leve som orme under overfladen. Rent sind, ren krop.
Tag det stille og roligt. Kærlighed, håb, overbærenhed, velvilje. Jeg kan ikke forklare hvorfor
det onde er ondt. Jeg tror nytteetik er nyttigt, men også kun nyttigt. Når alting flyder bliver
det svært at forklare, hvorfor dyr ikke skal dø. Med circle of life bliver det svært at finde
godt og ondt. Når man gerne vil transcendere dualismerne bliver det svært. Jeg skal i seng snarest,
for at gøre op.

Dit sind vil gå i stykker og forfalde, hvis du ikke holder det rent og simpelt. Du vil forfalde
til mærkelige mønstre. Det er ikke bare kognition, processeringshastighed og kapacitet, der er
afgørende, det er også det mere kvalitative. Jeg sad i dag og brugte lang tid på r/trashy, hvor
der var mange mærkelige ting. Der var en video med en kvinde, der råbte en masse grimme ting efter
en afroamerikaner, og det var tydeligt at se at hun ikke bare var ond men også var skadet i hjernen.
Det er ikke fordi jeg vil påstå, at der er en direkte korrelation mellem intelligens og godhed
overhovedet. Det handler nok mere om, at hvis vi skal blive gode, så skal vi kunne se os selv, så
skal vi besku os selv, og så skal vi være fri fra de dæmoner, der fanger os i sådanne mønstre,
og som gør os til noget vi ikke kan lide. Selvom jeg ikke var glad for, hvor meget tid jeg brugte
på den side, var der bare så mange eksempler på mærkelig menneskelig adfærd, at man også må
anerkende, at vi alle har potentialet. Kan jeg finde eksempler på ting i mit eget liv, hvor jeg
også bare handler og tænker på en irrationel måde, på en måde der udgår fra et sted, hvor der ikke
er ro?

Software development is a process in which large information processing systems is built.
Such an enterprise involves a variety of technologies as well as a plurality of human stakeholders.
Software development is concerned both with the technical aspects, such as object oriented
programming languages and testing technoloigies and with the other side which concerns
management, business, risks and costs etc. Most of it is placed somewhere in between.
Here we are concerned with general methods for building adaptive systems which can change
based on new requirements, which can be maintained easily and extended without needing excessive
time and will introduce new bugs. There is also the question of design, the way in which the
structure of the system is made. A structure can be more or less flexible and modular. Elements
and responsibilities are reasonable. Designers look at the problem domain and establish
concepts by recursive application of the object oriented analysis, in which actors, concepts,
processes and relations between concepts are identified. A big problem in the exposition which
has been given in the lectures at my university is the immense focus on the social institution
of software development as it exists in capitalist society. Here software development is always
discussed within a specific frame of reference in which the developer is working for a consultancy,
which is interaction with a client company, the customer. The requirements to the system comes
from the customer even though the technical and specific requirements is mostly made in
collaboration, because the customer company does not itself have the technical expertise needed
to formulate these.

We have been introduced to the waterfall model in which the steps involved in the development
of the system proceeds in discrete steps, with requirements, analysis, design, implementation,
and evaluation/testing appearing after each other.

Software. Software. I have not been fond of the word, the sound, the auditive texture. Software.
Software is an abstract entity with a material embedding. Software is code. Software is a bad
concept because it is hard to use linguistically. You have to say a piece of software in some
cases, but software does not come in pieces. A software. A software is an information processing
system which is designed not as a simple algorithm. It is a networked structure. It can be
running or it can be deprecated, active or in development. It has a design, a teleology, a
reason, it has a functionality, a behavior, a logic, a static and dynamic structure. It has
a use and a capacity. It has errors, it has movement and flow. It has control and policy. It
has users and developers, stakeholders. It has a coupling, it has a cohesion. It has objects,
modules, classes, interfaces, methods, variables, fields, properties, dependencies. It has
a lot. Software. I am not software, I have no software in my brain. Software is computational.
Software is in silico. Software. Why do I not have any idea what software is, why do I lack
the power to articulate fundamental knowledge about it? Software is made of code. Software
developers will try to solve a problem by recursively describing the problem domain by use
of discriminary and discrete thought which is linguistic. Through analysis of the problem and
the domain, a picture emerges which is a model. This model has a reality within the minds of
developers, designers and architects.

06-04-19-06-28
Nonlinearity biimplies feedback. Complexity biimplies nonlinearity. Feedback is hard to control
however. It is hard to ensure that the behavior of a nonlinar system is actually functional.
Since object oriented design is concerned with the construction of systems, how does the field
relate to these concepts?

Low coupling of the system means that the class structure is distributed and constitutes a
sparse network, where a classes is connnected to a limited set of other classes.
Since object oriented systems are modularly structured at different scales of organisation,
low coupling also regards the knowledge one component such as a class has about the inner
workings of other components. This knowledge should be limited. All external components should be
treated as abstract data types, with which we are not concerned with the internal implementation
but only behavior. Therefore the use of interfaces has the potential to decrease the coupling
of the system: If we use interfaces we are forcing ourselves to dealing with specifications of
behavior instead of implementation. 

Since the system has been teleologically constructed by software developers it has intended
functionality. This functionality does not arise as an emergent property but based on the
functionality of subsystems. Cohesion refers to whether the elements of the system relating
to specific subproblems are actually grouped together in the class structure. It would be
possible to have a low coupling in general but if this coupling was not a coupling to relevant
and related classes, then there would still be a problem. This cohesion is not fuzzy, based
on the clustering of the complete class structure. The system is divided into discrete modules.
Here it is possible to ask whether the capacities and functionality of the module belongs
together. Do they act in concert? A module has more than one behavior, but the behaviors should
be similar or related.

11-04-19-20-03
The human activity of playing a musical instrument is so supremely nervous, it involves the
establishment of deep patterns of detailed mechanical movement, which has to be practiced by
a forceful repetition. A pattern such as a scale is learned first as a visual image. On the
guitar it is of a the fretboard and gradually it moves into the fingers as movement. It is
not a matter of knowledge, as the player will be able to show the specific notes which are
part of the scale. Rather it is a matter of speed and of reflex. When asked to play the scale
at a specific speed, there is a probability distribution for each note and it is the job of
the training musician to refine these probability distributions for every note. There is no
such thing as pure perfection only very low probabilities of errors. When the player becomes
proficient at playing the scale up and down, they might move on to other kinds of exercises
which again are patterns of movement. How is it that the establishment of these new patterns
does not destroy the proficiency in the already existing patterns? It might also be the case
that this happens, but the nervous system is capable of distinguishing to the degree that it
has been trained for this task. It is important to notice that the while the nervous system is
involved, the movement of the fingers makes it a highly physiological activity which will put
severe strain on the tissue of the player. In this way the praxis of music exists in a very
special place within the matrix of physiology, neurology, cognition and directly the intellectual.

The process of improvisation involves the act of producing a seqeuence of notes which are not
specified beforehand, and the obvious question in this regard is how we are to view this structure.
We could say that if analysed closely it is to be modelled as a probabilistic Markov process,
in which that based on some history of notes, perhaps the last dozen of notes, there is a
probability distribution of moving to any other note and that this is it. However, even though
the intuitions we have about our own playing should not be trusted directly, we still have to
accept that they are very valid sources to involve in the uncovering of these processes. Among
the intuitions and language which we use, is the idea that there are motives and ideas which
are larger structures, which can constitute phrases. Furthermore there is the idea of tension,
which correlates with the idea of both a logic, necessity of the resolution. All of this points
to a general idea of a function which attributes not merely probabilities of future events but
a utility function; the player is able to evaluate the pleasure of the current situation and
based on this will try to predict which future movement will increase this tension and establish
a dynamic. In this way the improvisation can induce very strong altered mental states in the both
the player and other listeners because of the process seemingly builds a larger structure in
which the individual parts gain significance. 

Understanding these aspects of the process of practicing and improvising music is not merely
insteresting on its own terms, but also in relation to practice, improvisation, creativity and
virtuosity in general. There are fields where the process of practice is in some ways very
straightforward and so allow for both intense practice but also the establishment of flow
on the basis of continued feedback on the success of the practitioner but also continual
resistance or difficulty in this. Training scales and other patterns on the guitar always
involves the component of speed and so it is possible to always add more resistance. Chess
is another example of cases where it is possible to make algorithms which will allow the
practitioner to effectively train continually and manipulate the resistance. In other realms
such as mathematics and science and many other academic fields such as philosophy the process
of learning seems to be removed from this explicit nervous domain, making it hard to establish
a method for continual resistance. Mathematics has exercises and it is possible for the practioner
to get feedback. However, while this is the case, the exercises are constructed so that they
form a variety of classes in which the method is only applied in the same way continually with
little variance and no gradual resistance; instead the practioner moves onto another set of
exercises. The result is that the pracitioner can become proficient in solving these exercises,
but this is not the goal of mathematical practice. The phenomenon of exercises in this form
is only suited for learning to calculate, that is to use the simple tools which mathematics
contains. The art of mathematics however is an art of solving abstract problems and building
theory, exploring virtual territory, building arguments, structures of logical steps and
algorithms. Chess itself is a very pure mathematical structure, in which a simple set of
rules and a start position creates a vast tree of possible outcomes, just like the a set
of axioms can lead to a variety of propositions within logic. The difference is perhaps that
chess defines a goal and will be the task of the chess players to compute paths to this goal
in which the main complexity arises from the fact that there is uncertainty involved regarding
the actions of the opponent. More advanced mathematics books will contain exercises which ask
the student to prove various statements and so specify the goals in a manner which is reminicient
of the chess player's situation. These exercises are similar to the real practice of mathematics
because of the existence of conjectures. These conjectures have to be conjectured however, and
that happens on the basis of both curiousity and creativity. The act of conjecturing is one in
which the mathematician has a hypothesis, sees a pattern, a possibility but is not completely
sure that it is true. How can such a thing be the case? What does it mean that the mathematician
is a little sure? Is it an unconscious component of the mathematical mind which is able evaluate
some kind of importance, tension and release?

Musician will train phrases and licks with which can be included in an improvisation and this
phenomenon makes it clear that it is difficult to conceptualise improvisation as the unplanned,
because the lack of planning is only present at a specific level, a specific temporal horizon.
Chess involves strategies and openings. Mathematicians have proof techniques which are tools
with which they can build the proofs and different techniques will be tried out and perhaps
one tool will be more promising than another. From this it becomes clear how the act of proving
theorems is an empirical process and from the perspective of connectionism regarding cogntion,
it is hard to think of it in any other way. Automatic theorem proving is the idea of trying to
use computation to compute the proofs for theorems either both by probabilistic and
non-probabilistic means. This project is both interesting on its own terms but also as a means
for gaining a deeper understanding of what the mathematical art really is. One could imagine
futures where automatic theorems solvers play the role chess computers play today as a tool aiding
the training of human chess players.

In general, this whole discussion brings me a view to endeavour of human practice. We will have
to accept that we are not really special in the universal sense, that our physiological, neural,
cognitive and intellectual capacities are limited and specific and that there is no theoretical
fact which excludes the possibility of future systems which are superior on all fronts. Furthermore,
we are asked to view ourselves on the same terms, as learning systems in which the ability to
prove theorems, play chess, make art and improvise is not a result of deeper priciples but the
establishment of complex neural patterns which allow for advanced computation. In this light
there is a sense in which practice can seem quite futile since it has the likeness of rote
memorisation, even though this perspective is slightly off, since the goal is not memorisation
and originality can still exist even though it the roots of the original product can still be
traced. However, we can also choose to see ourselves as the most capable of all currently existing
computational systems. Accepting this fact should fill us with respect for ourselves and feelings
of responsibility. By praciticing various arts we are doing valuable work which cannot at the
current moment be done better by any other system. When we practice music, mathematics or chess
there is only a miniscule probability that we will become the best person on the planet but
this thought is a kind of error of thought since there is no reason why that should be the goal.
It is not enough that the knowledge of calculus or some other body of human knowledge is compiled
in hundreds of books by authors who will know the subject better than you ever will. The knowledge
is presented in these books because there is value in having many people know it to some degree
of proficiency, because this knowledge holds power: The knowledge can be applied in the creation
of technology, services, systems, evaluations and much more. By learning it you will attain of
the power within this knowledge and become more powerful yourself. One could argue that this is
not the case with music and chess, since they do not seem to have the same practical applicability
as academic knowledge or technical skills. I believe, however, that there is still space for these
activities, because they stimulate us and provide great joy. I certainly believe that the reason
why this entry has become so uncharacteristically long and coherent can be attributed to the fact
that I have just been practicing on the guitar which I have not done for many months.

10-04-19-11-42
Pascal's wager is special in the following way: It concerns hypotheses about the world.
These hypotheses have consequences of varying degree, that is there is a function which assigns
a scalar consequence (goodness or importance) if that hypothesis is true. Pascal's wager is
as much a theory of what to do with this probabilistic phenomenon: Pascal proposes a theory
in which you multiply the probability of the event with the concequence of the event. It is
merely a formal way of saying that we do not merely care to what degree we believe different
things to be the case; some things might be quite unlikely but if they were true they would
have major consequences. What is important? Does this way of thinking not become almost ethical?
At least in concerns values in some way. How does conditional probability figure into this?
Pascal's wager concerns a single event, namely Christianity. The event Christianity can either
be true or false. If it is true, it is multiplied by infinity by its consequence. As I understand
it, this inifinite consequence is the actual bliss received by the person accepting the bet, if 
he wins. Perhaps there is nothing new in everything I am talking about, it is merely a matter
of betting. It is a wager after all. But probability theory is hard, and every insight matters.
When we are thinking, as we always are, various hypotheses arise in our heads.

The entry into consciousness is a signal in an arbitrary number of dimensions. Surely it is very
structured, at least into the various senses, even though these senses may be confused.
Our grand question is this: The brain needs to be able to extract the importance, the consequences
of some aspects of the signal or the thought from those parts which are less so.
Is it the case, that there is a set of hypotheses held by the brain for the incoming signal?
These hypotheses would render the actual experience more or less likely, but they would also
render the experiences more or less important. It is this double-sided phenomenon, which I am
trying to wrap my head around. I should not dismiss myself as being too stupid. Every curious
thought, no matter how stupid, is okay. If you try to believe that you know it already, then
you will never learn. Look, the idea of humiliation is closley interlinked with the intellectual
project. I define the intellectual project as the endavour to gain simply gain knowledge, to
use the rational mind to learn and understand the world. The intellectual project is both
personal and collective: We as humanity strive to know and we collaborate in building this
vast base of knowledge and it is the hallmark of our civilisation, it is what defines it
and gives it its power, because of the strong correlation between power and knowledge.
It is also a personal project, but every person has their own priorities and might prioritise
the intellectual project as they see fit. Personally, I believe it to be very high on my
priorities, I see it as a fundamental goal of life, to strive for knowledge. I believe, however,
that this knowledge is to be used for effect on the world, specifically the increase of power
of the various organisms and systems of the world and in order to lessen the suffering which
correlates with this lack of power. I like how I have used the word "correlate", it is an easy
way to write, because you are not making any strong causal propositions. Everything which is
experienced, any thought which arises is based on correlation, and it is valid in that sense,
in the sense that there is a correlation. It is worth much that there is a correlation, since
the human brain is the most advanced of any statistical computational system. However, perhaps
here is a relevance for my reflections on the consequences: A thought arises to signify a
correlation between two phenomena, but it does not appear on its own, one has to "divide" by
the importance or the consequence for the organism if these two phenomena are connected.
On a related note, the number of citations of a scientific article denotes not the degree of
belief in the hypothesis it expounds (nice phase: to expound as hypothesis). Instead it is
a simple measure of the importance or the immediate consequence of this hypothesis.

There are some phenomena which are computationally hard, because the consequences of the various
hypotheses may be great. Social interactions are very computationally demanding, because every
bit of information received can be of great importance. I expounded (the hypothesis) that a
cause of the use of alcohol is that it sets a barrier (modelled as some function of resistance)
to the use of computational power involved in social interactions. Parties are the most extreme:
They are 10 hour windows in which as many and 20 people interact, constructing a huge network
of interactions. A single interaction: A person stands alone at the window and another person sees
it. This is an interaction, because information about one person is transmitted to another.
Very fast, the degrees of freedom rise. The only point of all this is really to say that the
computation involved in being in a party is considerable, and presuming the person has goals
such as being social, then putting a barrier on the computation will be a means of focus even
though we do not consider alcohol to be a means of focusing. Measuring the cognitive performance
of test subjects on the influence of alcohol in a lab setting will hardly be ecologically valid.

expectations but still I have a focus: Healing and connection with beauty, reconnection with
the body and its dynamic complexity. Reentering the sacred room with its symmetries. Expansion.

hold the capacity to inflict on us. I must not forget art, there is a danger that my world view
will become limited by its focus on information and mathematics that it will lose the power
the poetic mind. Grace. Graceful movement of the body is important because it calibrates the
mind. Nail biting is the least graceful of all movements because it is so specific and oriented,
yet it is far from the depths and goals of the higher mind. I need to accept that the brain is
a network of vastly different components and that while they all have their place, there are
some which are more noble than others. It is not a matter of distancing oneself from other animals
instead the human species is unique and its good sides should be magnified as should good sides
for any other system or phenomena. Peace to the world. I woke up this morning and felt the beauty
of the bird's song outside the window. It is a song because it was pleasant to me. I do not know
why it is pleasant. Does it connect to something deep within me? Does the origins of this signal
have a connection to some of my origins? I do not know. I can hear them now, and they are as
pleasant as ever. I can hear the sound of the keyboard, as my fingers glide over the keys. I
am thankful for having a machine, and I am thankful that such a habit has formed in my nervous
system which allows the production of these linguistic structures. Surely, language has an immense
beauty. Still it has its strengths and its weaknesses. The identifications of these are important.
There is language within me which lifts experience to a new level, because it is used to connect
the contents of consciousness into a larger frame where it gains beauty. There is also language
within me, however, which does harm. It would be good for me to learn more about cognitive
behavioral therapy. No judgement. One of the problems or issues with drugs is that they allow you
to experience beauty and peace (which you did not know you needed) but there is a tendency in
me to draw conclusion which abstract to the general life in which I am not under the influence.
Thus, I am interpreting the effects in the mind, which are thoughts which may seem wise or peaceful
as the cause of my peace instead of the effects of the chemistry and signal transduction. The
small insight which is rather a kind of admission, that the chemical effects have to be acknowledged
fully, can be seen as the difference between the transhumanistic viewpoint and the simple spiritual
viewpoint. By these viewpoints I mean that the transhumanist wants to alter the material biological
structure in order to improve the mind, the peace and the perfection of consciousness, while the
simple spiritual viewpoint views spiritual techniques such as meditation as being generally
sufficient for the process of perfecting the mind. There is a big difference, especially because
the transhumanist will not necessarily believe that this perfection can happen to themselves, but
that it may be possible some day in the future, while the simple spiritual view perhaps would
believe that all the tools were within reach even though the path may be very long. If both
viewpoints are held at the same time, to the degree to which the two viewpoints do not contradict
each other, then the person is faced with a task of prioritising. For the specific person, the
highest gains might be to focus on the spiritual practices but from the viewpoint of the whole
of humanity, the resources will perhaps be better invested by working for the advancement of
science and technology. I will meditate a bit now, I do not feel any strong effects even though
I do not expect to. The majorify of the molecules might have been on the other half of the blotter.

08-04-19-20-35
The smoke rose violently above his head. He had not seen the light fall on
it in such a way in any of his previous lives. He felt so sure but reprimanded himself for being
so. Feeling sure was not one of his ideals, quite the contrary.
He was one of those who kept his mind open
as a large tree where any bird could land and stay for a day or two. Ideas and beliefs were
nothing but toys for him and he treated them like shit. He abused them and did with them whatever
he liked. All of this happened beneath closed eyelids but suddenly he opened his eyes and the
smoke was gone. The sensations in his feet where silvery gray and the granularity was high, as
they say. Taking a deep breath, he was sure death was not going to come within the hour. It's all
about the heart, my friend. He had acquired the habit of speaking to himself as though a schism
had happened: Second person. He did not believe any voice within the mind to be himself, however,
and that was probably what saved him from many awful experiences. Instead they were nothing but
hypotheses, most of them so utterly retarded that if taken to represent him, he would have to
say goodbye.

Anxiously, he put his hands on the floor to assist his movement into standing position, like
a true erectus. He instantly began wildly biting his nails and fingertips. He did not hesitate,
he was not aware, he was not conscious. The whole system of the mouth attacked the fingers
like savage monsters with no regrets and no conscience. He believed that all pleasure, all
happiness and all fear could be felt within the body itself, that the mind was always spatial.
He received intense gratification from the barbaric destroyal of his hands but was confused by the
fact that he could not locate this joy within the body. That did not stop his endeavour the least.
Indeed, he was a true multitasker like the rest of us.

Spar mig, sagde han igen, men rundt om ham stod vi tavse. Tilliden til Yogma var alt for stor
til at jeg kunne frygte nu, det var ligesom for sent, valget skulle være taget for timer siden.
Lange tynde fingre med end endnu elastisk hud gned mod øjenlågene. Der var noget nærmest musikalsk
over måden han åndede ud og ind, det bragte mig i en stille trance, der bar mig det sidste kvarter.
Blandet med savl udgik der mærkværdige sætninger fra hans tunge, for eksempel ting som: Jamen dog,
hvordan har jeg kunnet leve uden. Eller: Hallelujah. Eller: Det er for godt til at være sandt.
Han rømmede sig altid inden. Måske fordi det krævede en kraftpræstation. Det blev ved i længere tid
end jeg havde forventet.

Jeg drømte at Ariana Grande spillede en sang på et klaver ude i entreen hjemme i Gjern på en sådan
måde at hun var dækket af en masse jakker imens. Jeg prøvede at fjerne nogle af dem, så hun ikke
var gemt sådan væk og overvejede, om hun var gift.

Jeg er så træt. Der er en blæser, der kører. Der kommer en inspektør eller pedel eller hvad han

vil gerne lære CBT, det virker spændende, det virker som om det giver mening at blande det med
mindfulness, fordi der så også kommer en analytisk side til selvbevidsthed.

Jeg var sammen med Jonas og Peter i går. Jeg cyklede herfra uden en mobil, fordi jeg glemte den
i bilen; vi kom fra Bornholm og de andre lige hurtig med oppe og sætte lampe op, men det skulle
gå hurtigt. Jeg cyklede i t-shirt og solen skinnede, og jeg cyklede ned ad Nørrebrogade, og jeg
tænkte, at sommeren er en slags parringstid, og at det er sjovt at der er sæsoner, og at det er
ærgerligt at vi er i en verden, hvor vi ikke altid er på toppen. Jeg tænkte, at der var noget galt
med mig, fordi jeg hele tiden forestillede mig at ansigterne på folk tilhørte folk jeg kendte.
Jeg cyklede ned til Studenterhuset, fordi jeg skulle have wifi, så jg kunne bruge min computer
til at vide, hvad Jonas og Peter havde aftalt. Studenterhuset var omdannet til et stort
tøjloppemarked. Jeg så kun piger. Jeg så en pige, der havde et kæmpe smil. Jeg så en anden pige,
der var rigtig smuk, men som også var meget ung. Jeg fandt ud af at, at vi skulle mødes hos Jonas.
Jeg cyklede videre. Jeg tænkte, at jeg ikke ville ryge med Jonas, fordi jeg har misbrugt cannabis
i marts, og at jeg ikke tror det gør mig noget godt. Jeg aftalte det med mig selv. Jeg cyklede
forbi Christianshavn og ned på Amager. Jeg cyklede uden mobil og jeg cyklede lidt forkert, nok
fordi jeg havde cyklet til Caroline og blandede det sammen.

Jeg kom frem og Peter var ikke kommet.
Jonas havde det godt, stille og roligt, søndagsvibes. Han havde groet svampe Cubensis som han
skulle tage i næste weekend med nogle venner. Han havde groet dem fra et kit, han havde købt,
som var let at bruge. Han havde spist noget inden, et par små for at mærke, hvad det var, men
det var på en onsdag. Han havde også spist en større, en gang inden en fest på CSS, hvor Benjamin
ellers havde wingman'et ham så meget. Han havde en ven, der havde groet mange flere svampe end
ham fra samme slags kit, og ham og hans ven havde spist dem alle sammen på en dag. Vi lå i hans
seng og snakkede, da Peter kom. Jonas viste ham svampene, og sagde at vi var i gang med at snakke
om dem. Jeg nævnte Terence McKenna, fordi jeg mener det er ham der lidt har startet fænomenet
med at gro svampe og at det også er Cubensis han skrev om i hans guide. Jeg fortalte om Tao Lin
og Trip. Vi pakkede nogle håndklæder og shorts og gik mod stranden imens vi talte om Terence
McKenna og DMT og andre ting. Jeg fortalte det med at McKenna havde sagt at han selv var
rationalist og materialist oprindeligt, men at det ændrede sig, da han tog DMT. Det talte vi en
del om; Peter mente at det var problematisk at tage det, hvis man ville ende med at tale med
aliens resten af livet, selvom man måske ville synes at verden var mere interessant. Da vi
nåede stranden skiftede samtalen ved association til at handle om en South Park episode, hvor
"japanerne" kom og nakkede delfinerne og hvalerne i Sea World.

handling the tools right, not whether it is computationally possible.

Try to become better at looking at documentation, that is what the intelligent people do,
they try to understand the minds of their creators. I should also become better at writing
documentation for my own stuff, because it as interesting linguistic exercise, the engineering
part, the report style, the conciseness. Very different from this style. Programming is
linguistic exercise, but it operates with a Turing Machine and not a context-sensitive grammar,
thus there are many more rules and the rules can be almost completely arbitrary. As I am
learning to operate Python3 and the related relevant it requires memory. I have to remember
how to do stuff, I have to rememeber the syntax. It is as if though there is difference here
compared to natural language. In natural language the syntax is easy to learn from chomskyan
perspective, the same goes for NLP. It is semantics which are difficult. Where does it become
hard? I don't know how to completely express my own ideas, because I do not have any programming
language in which I am fluent. It seems as though the idea of fluency is very hard to describe
when it is not strictly at the level of natural language. Look at what I am writing now, you
could make a simple threshold for writing and claim that this is fluency. Mostly fluency is
thought of as relating merely to operating second tongues. But programming languages are very
much second or third tongues. Programming, the third tongue. I like the sound of that. If we
argue that there are ideas which are prior to the specific grammars of a given language, that
I can have some kind of intention when I am writing, that there is some meaning which could
have been formulated in another way, then what? There is a fluency to thought too; it seems
as though a lack of ideas will result in a lack of fluency. It is difficult to talk about the
fluency. Verbal fluency, look at that. Stammering is an example; you mostly have an intended
sentence, but it is not getting expressed, articulated at the level of tongue.

29-03-19-09-21
Glæde er et centralt komponent i den generelle magt. Magt er et større begreb end glæde, fordi
det går ud over sindstilstande alene og inkluderer kompleksitet og kunnen. Ideen om frygt-magt
er et alternativ til parret svaghed-magt. Hvis glæden er forbundet med magt er det både frygten
og sorgen, der er en svaghed. Den glade står over den anden. Det er freaken, der går med et
kæmpe smil på panden ned ad gaden, der er magtfuld, fordi han ikke som den svage bliver trukket
ned af verdens grimhed. Verdens grimhed er en udfordring. Den magtfuldes smil er ikke et resultat
af en sindstilstand som sådan, det er ikke et svar på en positiv hændelse. Den magtfulde er ikke
den person, for hvem det går godt, og som et resultat af dette er glad. Den magtfulde har et
smil, der er genereret så det står i zenith til en smerte. Smilet er ikke sarkastisk, men det er
stadig trodsende. Det trodser ikke andre mennesker. Det er lige præcis det overdrevne fokus på
andre mennesker, der trækker folk ned og gør dem svage. Gentænkelsen består ikke i at løsrive
sig fra socialitet som sådan, men i at anerkende socialitetens plads i det større billede. Derfor
kommer magt ikke uden en mængde koldblodet rationalitet, der vejer de sociale strukturer ud fra
en længere temporal horisont.

28-03-19-16-45
Evolution is fundamentallly a computer scientific concept, it describes the dynamics of
information replication. The world is full of wonderful objects and systems which are waiting
to be described. It is a creative and productive activity which is required to look at these
things, describe them, apply theories. Model two people speaking. They are interaction through
the auditory signals. Information processing in two separate brains, two tongues. We need to
look at them as as entities in a grander system of langauge as it is practiced. When we are
thinking we are conjuring algorithmic models. A part of this work is the brainstorming which
I am doing now; a rouch flow of ideas which are connected on the fly. But writing plays a large
role for me know, because it seems as though my thinking is largely linguistic. It is interesting
however, that it is not based on speaking. I am speaking to some people, I have had good talks
with Carl, Axel, Jacob, Caroline and Oskar, Steven and other people.

Literature is a concept which at the surface does not relate to computer science. However,
literature in general can be viewed as a set of documents, which can be represented digitally.
As soon as something can be represented digitally it is open to the surface of the computational
virtual strata. I have completely forgotten my older texts and I do not wish to spend time on
it now. Literature a timeline of texts. Philology appears as a kind of lower technical
Wissenschaf, which is relevant to the synoptic gospels I have been thinking about. I have not
been able however to present any convicing way of applying algorithms to the synoptic gospels
as digital strings. I have moved onto Google Maps data, in which I have not progressed any further
than producing a Python dataframe with longitude, latitude and timestamp. For Firefox I have
found the websites I have been to, and they will become another temporal variable in a future
model that I do not have the technical ability to construct yet. Here we will have to try to
find out how to measure the dynamics of webactivity at a point in time within relation to the
past as a fading horizon. There is certainly something like a function that models frequency.
What is frequency? It is the number of occurences within a window. How many sites per hour?
The problem with Markov chains is that they do not include enough temporal memory, they do not
think in frequencies. How many words is my sentence? It should be easy to count the most simple
frequency as all the words divided by the sentences. This average could also be dynamically
calculated. In general it does not seem to be the interesting thing algorithmically.

How can we unthink!? Unthinking happens by forgetting, but is there a way to do this which does
not include a destroyal of the cogntivie capacities of the one who tries to think again. I
realize, that I have to take the idea of ideas seriously as something to describe rigorously.
Rigour is the hall mark of science, and it is computational modeling which is the finest and
purest of methods for combining the deductive and inductive, the mathematical and the empirical.

I believe I do not yet have the sufficient toolkit in terms of understanding data structures.
For example I would like to gain a deeper insight into the data structure Git uses, Merkle Trees,
Blockchains and so on. There is a deep use of hashing. I had a very nice experience of solving
a problem in the Discrete Math and Algorithms DMA course where a sorted list of numbers is
searchable to find the specific percentile. Here the list is turned into leaves of a tree with
their parents recursively summing the numbers all the way to a root. In the project of the
Markov chain I have used the Hoffman Algorithm which combines a similar method. Instead of my
method which would involve $\Theta(log n)$ search, the Hoffman has a variable length coding
which also means a variable length search time. The Hoffman algorithm is slightly information
theoretic in its origin, but it is easy to feel completely free in this regard and just interpret
it from that viewpoint. We are having an experiment. A data base. The data base is always
empirical. What do we have? We have the distribution of edges going out of the node onto the
following word. We do that because it is the simplest of all "statistical" ways of characterising
the data, not because we expect anything interesting in terms of generative modelling of
language. Who believes that it would ever be possible to look at language as just patches of

27-03-19-10-15
Post-PC era interaction, Aske Mottelson
March 27th 2019

lollern

Forskningsaktiviteter der foregår i HCI og som er relevant for de mere grundlæggende principper
fra kurset. Formålet er at sparke lidt til interessen for feltet og vise nogle af de cutting-edge
ting der foregår, som går udover mere grundlæggende ting.

Første time vil jeg gennemgå "mobile sensing", et paradigme, hvor man bruger datakilder fra fx
mobilen til at give ekstra information. Brugergenerede data til at give information til brugeren.

Anden time vil handle om VR-forskning, først body-ownership illusions, man prøver at ændre folks
opfattelse af deres krop og måder at agere med verden. Ingeniør-problemer, hvordan laver vi
for eksempel berøring.

Det er måske nogle store emner at gennemgå på så kort tid, og de overlapper måske ikke så meget,
men det er de emner jeg forsker i. Til sidst vil vi se videoer med publikationer fra det sidste
år, om hvordan VR bliver mere right.

Mobile sensing kan tænkes ud fra applikationer som Maps, hvor vi bruger sensorer som GPS til at
give ekstra information til brugeren. Sundhedstrackeren i iOS bruger accellerometer og gyrometer
som kan bruges til at beregne, hvor meget man har gået, hvor mange skridt. Den bruger en statistisk
model til at udregne det og give brugeren mulighed for at tracke sin fysiske sundhed over tid.
Det man prøver på, er at udvide det fra de fysiske sensorer til mere mentale og kognitive aspekter.
Koncepter som humør og følelser er mere komplicerede at kvantificere end hvor mange kilometer du
har gået. Forskellige datakilder bliver integreret. Helt basalt kan man forestille sig, at hvis
man gerne vil finde ud af om folk er stressede kan det være de bevæger musen mere. Man vil gerne
hjælpe folk til at fokusere osv. Det der generelt sker i ID-feltet er øget fokus på kognitive
funktioner i forhold til tidligere, hvor det mere var fysiske metrikker.

Hvordan kan man bruge mobildata til at finde folks følelser? Fruit Ninja spillet hvor man skal
skære frugt der falder. Hvis man tager detaljerne i swipet, hvor lineært det er for eksempel.
Hvor afslappet er du? Hvor meget keder du dig? Du kan lave statistisk korrelation mellem disse
følelser og information i swipet. Den måde vi interagerer med apperater siger noget om hvordan
vi har det. Det er også blevet brugt på stemmeføring, intonation, kompleksitten af sætninger.
Hvis folk er stressede taler de på ene anden måde. Man kan også gøre det med passiv data, hvor
brugeren ikke er aktiv: Der er lavet forskning, hvor man bruger baggrundsdata, for eksempel hvilke
apps man bruger, hvor lang tid man bruger, rækkefølgerne i aktivitet osv. kan være korreleret med
mental helbred. Disse kræver ikke så mange apperater som hvis vi skal måle hjerte, sved osv.

Kan interaktionsdata være udslagsgivende for løgnagtighed? Studiet har tre eksperimenter.
En android-app. Der er forskellige grunde til at folk taler sandt eller ikke, på baggrund af
det laver vi en binær model for om folk er sandfærdige eller ikke. Mennesker lyver meget, måske
har du en økonomisk motivation til at lyve. Det er svært at vide. Mennesker er meget dårlig til
at gætte om folk lyver. Et studie, hvor folk der ikke kender hinanden skal give et udsagn, der
er sandt eller ikke. Folk har 54% accuracy is at gætte om folk lyver eller ej, når der er 50-50
a priori. Så de er moderat bedre end at slå plat eller krone.

Løgn i digital kommunikation kan bruges til at finde spam eller fake reviews. Typisk vil man lave
sproganalyse. Når folk lyver bruger de som regel mere komplekse ord, der er også nogle bestemte ord
der forekommer hyppigere. Der er også løgn, der ikke involverer prosa, for eksempel checkboxes osv.
Studiet bruge interaktionsdata, hvor på skærmen klikker du, hvor meget af fingeren brugte du,
hvor hurtigt svarede du. Tre studier der repræsenterer 3 forskellige paradigmer for løgn, 3 android
apps, brugere fra Amazon's Mechanical Turk.

Er der forskel på at lyve med en knap og en slider. Der er et paradigme om at løgn er en kognitiv
process af Williams et al. PLOS One '13. Hvis du skal lyve skal du tænke; du skal finde på en
case, der er konsistent. Det tager længere tid at lyve end at fortælle sandheden. Ideen med at
lave den første app var at replikere de resultater med en app. De statistiske resultater visser at
løgnen i gennemsnit tager længere tid for alle interaktionsformerne.

Within subjects design experiment er et forsøg, hvor alle deltagere har samme rolle, til forskel 
fra within subject design. Er folk tilbøjelige til at klikke længere ude på knappen? Hvor mange
gange har de klikket OK? Mere komplicerede er key dynamics; dynamikker i indtastning af tal, lidt
svært med så korte input, kun 2 cifre. Men generelt for key dynamics: Hvordan kan man vide, når
jeg logger ind, at det er mig? Hvor hurtigt taster jeg kodeordet, eller mere komplekse modeller
for min måde at taste kodeordet.

Folk har sjældent muligheden for at få penge ved at lyve på den her måde. Det er en del af konceptet
at folk har en måde at lyve på. I eksperiment 2 skal man ikke have lige så meget mulighed for at
lyve. Man bruger ofte terningekast. Forskning fra Aarhus Universitet, hvor man tager studerende
ind i et klasselokale for sig selv, sætte en streg for hver gang man slog en sekser og får nogle
penge for hver gang. Hvilke studieretninger har højere end 1/6 chance for en sekser?

I Yatzy er man rimelig motiveret til lige at ændre lidt. Betalte folk baseret på, hvor godt de
gjorde det.

Bond & DePaulo '06 viser at mennesker kan gætte løgn med 61% og løgne med 47%. I ultimatum-app
og yatzy-app, kan det de klassificeres bedre, men ikke overvældende.

Virtual reality
HCI indkorporerer mange forskkelige videnskabelige felter, jeg repræsenterer den mere tekniske
ende, idet jeg prøver at lave software og statistiske modeller, hvor interaktion er et matematisk
fænomen. Jeg har prøvet at lave nogle nedslag i den mere tekniske ende af HCI. Nu har i hørt om,
hvordan man kan koble mobilinteraktioner og kognitive processer. Virtual reality er nærmest kedeligt
populært i HCI, næsten halvdelen af de papers der bliver præsenteret på konferencer.

Microsoft Research er nærmest som et universitsforskning, men det er lidt mere anvendt. 

Helt fundamentalt er der et kontinuum af forskellige virkelighedsrepræsentationer i den her
teknoloig. Helt til venstre er den virkelige verden, helt til højre er det helt virtuelt miljø,
dine egne sanser er erstattede af computergenerede grafik og lyd. I mellem disse ender er
der augmented virtuality, hvor der taget elementer fra den virkelige verden ind i den virtuelle
verden, eller augmenteret reality, hvor det hovedsageligt er reality med virutelle elementer.

1968: Sword og Damocles var det første projekt der minder om VR, minder konceptuelt meget om
VR-headsets. 1985 lavede Jaron Lanier nogle suits, ideen var at man kunne bruge til at træne
astronauter osv., ordet VR blev opfundet. 1991 blev det mere tilgængeligt for forbrugere, men
der var ikke rigtig nogen producenter, der lavede spil, folk blev søsyge.

I 1999 kom Matrix, 2003 kom Second Life. VR kom ind i offentlige medier

2012: Crowdfunding $2.5m oculus, købt af Facebook. Løst mange problemer med søsyge.
HTC, Oculus, Google, CAVE2.

Det er ikke kun i spilindustrien, det har skabt interesse. Især i HCI med fokus på menneskets
opfattelse af dets krop er der kommet et boom. 

Foreløberne i undersøgelsen af body ownership illusion er psykologer og neurovidenskabsfolk.
Helt mørkt rum, refleksive prikker på kroppen, kameraer kan se det; når du bevæger dit ben
bevæger dit ben sig også.

Banakou et al. 2013. Between-subjects: Halvdelen får barnekrop, halvdelen får voksenkrop i
barnestørrelse. Ownership illusions, så man bliver overbevist eller immersed.
Man kan måle ud fra spørgeskemaer, hvor meget body ownership man føler. Ideen om at man kan overføre
body ownership er baseret på 90'ernes rubber hand illusion. Visuomotor synchrony mapping mellem
sansning og perciperet sansning. Det er det samme man gør i VR, bare mere udvidet version.

Hvor stor tror du en boks er? Dem der har barnekrop estimerer boksen til at være større. Hvis
man tror man er et barn, tror man at ting er større. Den forskel findes ikke når du har en
voksenkrop. Folk bruger også simplere ordforråd efter at have været i barnekrop, underbevidste
processer. Der er en sammenhæng mellem den krop vi har og vores tanker: Hvis du har en rygsæk
med sten på vil du estimere antallet af trin på en trappe til at være højere. Med disse
between-subject studies kan du zoome ind på disse features.

Tai-chi, hvor man har forskellige kroppe; kaukasisk, sort, asiatisk og sammenhæng med implicit
racial bias. Hvis du har haft en sort krop har du haft en nedsat racistiske forudantagelser.
Ideen er, at man kan studere hvordan kroppen relaterer til sind. Fordi VR er blevet billigere
og virker bedre, så der blevet lavet utroligt mange studier. Det er med til at udvide vores
psykologiske viden.

Microsoft Research. RoomAlive. Bruger projektor og kamera til at lave 3d model af værelse ved
kalibrering.

Et problem for room-scale VR. Den virtuelle verden vil altid være større end et 25 kvadratmeter
værelse. Den mest benyttede måde til at udvide, er at du kan telepotere. Problemet med at
telepotere, er det ekstremt forvirrende at være et helt nyt sted og det giver søsyge. Det
at gå på stedet giver den samme søsyge. I redirected walking manipulerer man det bevægelsen
en smule. Hvis der er for meget rotation for hurtigt. Rotere hver gang man lukker øjnene.

Viden om øjnene bruges til optimere den virtuelle verden. Give små stimuli, der øger antallet
af blink.

Det er utilfredsstillende at interagere med en verden, hvor der ikke er haptisk feedback.
Der er forskellige forskningsprojekter, der prøver at understøtte det.

I have analysed the occurences and frequencies of characters in this document using mar23b.py.
There are 98 different characters. There are 244771 characters in total. The entropy of the
distribution is 4.4242 out of a maximumum 6.6147. I have installed the NetworkX python library.

I have made a graph in which words are nodes and they are connected if they occur in the same
sentence. Number of nodes: 7883. Number of edges: 259740 Number of components: 83
I have one giant component with 7780, the rest are sentences with one or two words in them.

Having multiple components is a simple way to have an analyzable topology. Thus one might
try to increase the number of components and the distribution of their sizes, for example
by using only parts of sentences split by comma. One could also drop this approach and start
by looking further at the giant component. Presumably there are some words which have very
large in degrees.

24-03-19-18-46
One idea for analysing flexibility and newness of information in the log entries could be
to first establish a graph of all words with edges between words which appear in the same sentence
as a crude indicator of similarity. There would be two different weight functions on the edges,
the first would be the number of sentences k, in which the two words appear together. The second
could be -log(k/M) with M being the total number of words. This idea is based on assignment 11
from the DMA course. For two edges a and b with k_a > k_b, -log(k_a/M) would be smaller than 
-log(k_b/M) this means that we can use idea of shortest paths for such a weight function. When
finding a shortest paths in this way we still don't want to add unecessary edges, but we are
using the edges which have the highest k. My idea was that for a new paragraph where we want
a measure of newness, a minimal spanning tree would be constructed using the information weights.
Then it might be that the sum of the weights of this MST could be used as a measure in some way.

I have just plotted the distribution of words and the distribution is very uneven. This fact has
big importance to the way in which these graphs and measures are constructed.

What should we try to do? There seems to be an obvious reason to analyse my own textual production
under the notion of mutual information and flexibility. If I am to evaluate my own textual
linguistic productions, I should be interested in estimating whether there is an addition of
information in a new section, and whether I am generally on a path of development a change of
landscape and an increasing overall coverage of the whole terrain of possible reflection.
Even more, we should be able to analyse the relative structure that arises as more parts of
the world is included into the system. What is needed for such a project is a large enough
base of data, thus I may have to change my relation to having this log. I should actively try
to write in it, even though I do not have any inspiration, so as to provide a better and more
realistic data set. My own log and my analysis should be a prototype of a more general system
and a creative conception of a new mode of enhancing the crystallised intelligence of human
beings. It may also prescribe a specific praxis, one in which the user is encouraged to interact
with the system. The goal is the establishment of a machine system which trains the user in the
production of information rich and complex text. Even though me might have criciticms of the
kind of elitism of such an intellectualistic training, in which the vocabulary could seem 
unnecessarily wide and the scope of discourse likewise extravagant, I believe that the user will
easily be able to distinguish between such a practice as writing in a log and everyday use of
language. Still, I hope for a world in which our conversations are deeper, more reflected, more
collaborative and more informed by reflection. My mother has noted that my use of notebook is
my version of the simple practice of contemplating in the mind. I do believe however, that there
is a great importance in the act of formulation, in the act of storing thoughts and pretending
to work. Not enough of us are doing intellectual work, in the sense that we believe our thought
to hold enough value to be really significant in the history of thought.

Now I will describe more clearly some ideas for how such a technological system should be built:
I have a text file here called log. This file is read into Python or F#. Here a single day note
can be treated as a separate object. The string is split into words. There is a finite number of
unique words appearing with a finite frequency. From this different random variable can be produced.
Either only the words within the paragraph or with relation to the full base of words. It seems
as though an interesting data structures could occur.

First you read in the whole file, establish all the words an their frequency. You perhaps order
them in a way in which they are highly accessible, in a hash table dictionary. Then you have also
the total number of words in the log.

think it would be fantastic to have that data, to know basic medical data about myself always. It
is not merely that I worry about my own body, my soma, I also desire it for the world population.
I desire that we believe in a future where that is the case for everyone. It requires resources
and we are in no direct hurry; we may need to get decarbonized first, but afterwards. I read an
artice from Effective Altruism cite which interestingly also discussed Lomborgs Copenhagen
